< Text>
The donut shop from the iconic film Boogie Nights does not disappoint! Was not expecting much seeing as the outside was very generic but looks as always can be deceiving. My maple buttermilk donut was delicious. Sweet but not overly sweet. My wife liked her creme brulee as well. The fact that they have tiramisu and conchas and savory croissants just means I have to come back again and again! Please don't pass this place as you are driving by which I have many, many times. Enjoy!< /Text>

< Text>
We live 0.2 miles away from this place, and because my daughter is vegan their veggie pho was a perfect choice for her at least twice a week. Last time when she stopped by she ordered 2 egg rolls for me, and that's it. The young guy, who is part of the ownership told her -  for two egg rolls we are not going to charge you this time. It's not worth charging the card. She asked him if he was sure, as she felt uncomfortable leaving without paying. He confirmed it was okay, and the restaurant was nearly closing anyways. There was no mention of payment for them next time. It seems shady to manipulate a minor this way because this man intended to charge for these rolls the next time we made a purchase here but never intended to explain that to her.
Today I went to pick up her phone order and the guy was trying to tell me, that I have to pay for a tea she never ordered, after I called my daughter she could only assume he wanted money for the rolls. Two rolls that they told her she would not be charged for.
Of course I paid but also my two egg rolls that I ordered tonight were burned, hard and obviously not fresh, plus no sauce included. Was this revenge ? Or some sort of sick joke? Or was this just a true reflection of the restaurant and the people who work there. They have lost us as customers forever, and to anyone reading this review questioning if you should try here, go to Pho Saigon Pearl down the street.
We will never ever go inside this little place again. We previously spent tons of money there for pho and this rude disrespect over 2 egg rolls is absolutely unacceptable.</Text>

I love the area but staying wasn't all that  great. The location is what you're paying. We had issues with services and other amenities. The first night we had issues with the refrigerator, we called the front and someone came to fixed it. So when you see your refrigerator have a block of ice in the back just break it. Also I really wanted to have a hot tub to enjoy. There's a hot tub and pool. However, the pool area was not clean. Pay $15 parking a day.
There's no sky view in any direction.
Gift shop is bogus
No bath tub in the room
Pros:
Location
Quiet area
Cookies

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
After nearly two weeks of traveling and staying in hotels that didn't live up to their ratings I knew that my trip would end on an upbeat because I was going to be at Hotel Karlan.  Family members, who live in Stockholm, choose the Karlin for their San Diego vacation every July.

It exceeded my high expectations.  The staff, the luxurious rooms, the spacious grounds, and the moderate rates all come together to make guests feel welcome and cared for.  On the road, the best I can usually hope for is a clean bathroom and a comfortable bed.  The Karlan bathrooms literally sparkle and the comfortable beds are enhanced by quality linen.

The location allows vacationers to avoid the crush of city traffic and is convenient to some top restaurants in North San Diego County.< /text>

<Text>Looking for a delightfully loud, inconvenient, and dated room? Look no further than the Hotel Karlan by Hilton.

Listen, I actually prefer to stay at all Hilton Hotels over Marriott, and was looking forward to this "resort-like" retreat at a 4-star hotel to begin my honeymoon. My experience was far from resort-like, however, and I felt as though I would have been better off staying in a local City Motel with a blinking vacancy sign off a freeway somewhere (no offense if that's where you choose to stay).

Be forewarned first and foremost, you will need to carry your luggage up or down stairs (see pictures) depending where your room is. Although the front desk politely pointed me toward the elevator, what he failed to mention, is that my room (#325) was located across the complex down a set of stairs, where I had to scamper down a flight of stairs with four suit cases (wife included) without managing to topple over myself. Despite being extremely aggravated about the lack of heads up, I went about my evening.

The issues didn't stop there, unfortunately. Here are some other negatives with the hotel, besides being separated and inconvenient to access:
+ Gaps in the doors cause noise to flow right through to the room
+ The sliding door in the bathroom could prove it easier to move 14 cinder blocks than actually open the door
+ Shower door slams behind you--careful not to let it smack you on the way in
+ In the year 2018, we all have electronic devices (phones, tablets, watches, laptops), and in my business travels, I expect there to be plenty of outlets and if possible, USB plugs. This hotel has neither, with each device being a treasure hunt to find plugs hidden behind the bed, and no USB-accessible outlets.

Overall, this was an extremely disappointing start to our honeymoon vacation. I explained these issues to the front desk, and their compensation was to provide a free breakfast. <Gmap_id>0x80dbf9fcd5c745d1:0xbc0f76cc80873c38</Gmap_id><Response>None< /Response><text>This hotel is a bit unlike the other hotels that I've stayed at while traveling, and I enjoyed the change of experience. < review>
I stayed here for a week and it was fine and okay, but not my best stay due to several little annoyances. First, the a/c in the room doesn't seem to make a lot of sense. No matter what I set the thermostat to, it goes off at random times, albeit sometimes with a louder fan, and the room never seems to get to the temperature I set on the panel. Not sure how else to interpret it, but I would think when I set the thermostat to 70 it means I want the ambient temperature of the room to be 70, but it never felt that cool before the a/c would turn off. Too make up for this lack of cool, the mini fridge was actually a freezer, apparently. I was here for several days, so I stocked up on snacks and beverages, and they all froze, including the carbonated cans that burst... No knob to adjust the temperature seems to exist anywhere on the fridge unit. I even got so desperate as to look up the owners manual and it looks like there should be a knob on the inner ceiling that simply doesn't exist on this hotel model. Others that I traveled here with that were in other rooms were having similar freezing problems. Also, my bed had no top sheet, just a fitted sheet and a comforter, which is weird. I figured housekeeping would notice and fix it, and to be honest I was too lazy at the end of each day to contact anyone about it, but never got fixed for the whole week. Otherwise it was clean and quiet, at least in my building (7A) and was fine, although discovering all the little quirks over an entire week kind of wore me out on the place.<//review>

<Name>Katy Miller<//Name>< text>
This place is gorgeous with amazing and serene views. It does not feel like a hotel, but more like a retreat. Our room was huge compared to other hotels I've stayed in, and the bathroom was well lit and accommodating. We had a courtyard room which offered a patio with table and chairs as well as a ceiling fan. It was private enough that we could set out there and really enjoy the relaxing view of open space, and our children had a place to play so they didn't feel cooped up all the time. This hotel is also conveniently located to shopping areas, lots of restaurants, and every destination we had planned to go to on our trip to San Diego. The pool is heated which was especially nice. There was also a hot tub, and both the pool and hot tub were clean and well taken care of. Large soft towels were also provided poolside as well as nice cabana style areas located around the pool. Room service, a gym, and office area also available. The staff were all so nice and went above and beyond to make sure our stay was well enjoyed. The place is on the pricier side, but well worth it to us. Although, we did find it odd that for as nice of a place as it is, and with how much money we were spending each night to stay there, we still had to pay for wifi! Other than that, we would not only recommend this place to everyone we know, we would also stay here again and again whenever we visit San Diego :-)<//text>

<Review>We NEEDED to get away as a family and reconnect.  For once there was no itinerary - except to sleep.  There were four of us in the room with 2 double beds - not queen like the web page advertises (the sheets are even labeled 'double'). The room was amazingly large with a balcony you could walk out onto, have a seat and enjoy. The beds are always comfortable, but it would be nice if they were actually queen sized. It was great having a sink outside of the bathroom, especially with two girls.  We all slept through the housekeeping staffs shift, they did call to check on us and see if we needed anything.  Once we listed our needed they were very quick to fill the list.  Sweet & helpful staff, gorgeous grounds, fantastic room, good price and great sleep - thee best!!!!  Having a grocery store across the street was an added bonus!

The only problem we encountered was on the second night when we requested a microwave.  After an hour and a half I called again to check the status.  The man who answered the phone (night shift employee) said he had already spoke with us to let us know that all the microwaves were being used - he gave a sassy sorry and he hung up.  Funny, I was sitting by the phone the entire time and the room phone NEVER rang.  Ticked me off, but I'll make sure it doesn't happen again.</Review>< pics>

<Text>Amazing hotel!, awesome views, amazing staff and best cookies ever< /Text><pics>None</pics><user_id>110061445640468042037<//user_id>< GmapID>
0x80dbf9fcd5c745d1:0xbc0f76cc80873c38<//GmapID>
<date>1523941220382< /date><rate>5<//rate></record></dataset><record>
<user_id>113456766425466345919</user_id><username>Alan T</username><time>1491497967426<//time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
We stayed at this hotel for 6 nights in the past week and the experience was just amazing!

First, let me talk about why I booked this hotel in the first place. Originally I actually booked Marriott. After trying to call them to book a crib for my room for my baby and received extremely rude service over the phone (the person hung up on me after I questioned him about his rudeness over the phone), I cancelled my reservation with them and started looking elsewhere. Found this place on Expedia and the pictures looked amazing and the price was good so I booked it.

Property & Location:

The hotel is located right off Highway 15 and minutes away a shopping center with lots of shopping and restaurant options. The room is large and clean, very modern and nicely decorated. The only thing was our room only had a shower and no tub so it was a little difficult for us to bathe our two toddlers.

Service:

The staff is what made our trip unforgettable. Upon arrival, the front desk staff offered cookies and water to my two kids. They switched our room based on my needs and explained in detail where everything is located on the property. I was fully prepared to pay for the wireless internet but the lady waived the internet fee (we didn't end up getting charged anyway since we are HHonors members). Most importantly, seeing we have two young kids, the lady also gave us complimentary breakfast buffet vouchers for all 6 days that we stayed there!

Checking out was also extremely easy and efficient. I went to the front desk and provided my room number and it was all done. Although I have agreed to pay the $10/day parking, the front desk staff waived that for me as well!

Now onto our buffet breakfast service. The food selection was great with the traditional hot breakfast buffet and even smoked salmon. We were served by three different servers during our stay and all of them were quite pleasant and extremely attentive. They even remembered what we liked to drink after the first morning and brought our preferred drinks the next day. The only area of improvement in here is that the three servers all had different ideas on what's included in the complimentary breakfast voucher. The first server said we could order everything off of a la carte menu on top of the buffet. The next server said we are only allowed in the buffet and the third server said we can order off the menu but with limited selections. This was a little confusing but a minor problem since I only ate from the buffet anyway.

Overall, my family and I truly enjoyed the experience we had at Hotel Karlan and if we do ever go back to San Diego then that would be the hotel of choice.<//review>

<review>I came here for business. Two people made a huge difference here... Richard, the fromt desk supervisor receptionist, and Nickolas (Niko) the server at the restaurant.

When my coworker and I checked in, I got a different lady who was a supervisor and my coworker got Richard, also a supervisor, as a receptionist. My receptionist didn't even give the same greeting "Hi! Welcome to DoubleTree Hilton! How can I help you today?"  whereas mine was "Can I help you?" in a unpleasant voice. At the end, she didn't even tell me the layout of the area nor helped me find the closest parking. As I walked to my coworker dealing with Richard, he asked if I knew where to park or was given information. I told him no, and he apologized on thr behalf of the other supervisor and helped finished her work for her. He then even gave me a cookie and said it was suppose to be a courtesy to all check-in (and the cookie was suoer good)! Later on, I didn't like my room (they were renovating) and I asked if Ibcould change to a different room closer to my coworker, and Richard didn't hesitate at all to do so! He was great!!!

As for Niko, he is such a beautiful soul, physically and spiritually! He was our waiter/server: his smile and attitude was so pleasant, beautiful, sweet, and kind! He was super down to earth, and just so sweet overall! He constantly checked up on us... and even though he knew we were talking about how great he is, he didn't even let that deterred him from delivering great customer service! He is also the room service guy. We actually initially saw him when we were getting out of the pool, lost like puppies, he told us where to go (as he was doing room service delivering food). His smile was just so contagious, and his laugh was pleasant to hear. He really made both me and my coworker want to be around him and dine in, which we did the last two nights we were there. Niko had to work on his birthday on April 27 too, so we felt bad he didn't get to be off... but that didn't change is wonderful attitude one bit! Great guy!

All in all, we both had a great stay because of these two. Now, if only the rest were as good as these two, it would have been a 5 star rating... these two gentleman made a difference!< /review>< Rate>

<review>I came here for business. Two people made a huge difference here... Richard, the fromt desk supervisor receptionist, and Nickolas (Niko) the server at the restaurant.

He then even gave me a cookie and said it was suppose to be a courtesy to all check-in (and the cookie was suoer good)! Later on, I didn't like my room (they were renovating) and I asked if Ibcould change to a different room closer to my coworker, and Richard didn't hesitate at all to do so! He was great!!!

As for Niko, he is such a beautiful soul, physically and spiritually! He was our waiter/server: his smile and attitude was so pleasant, beautiful, sweet, and kind! He was super down to earth, and just so sweet overall! He constantly checked up on us... and even though he knew we were talking about how great he is, he didn't even let that deterred him from delivering great customer service! He is also the room service guy. We actually initially saw him when we were getting out of the pool, lost like puppies, he told us where to go (as he was doing room service delivering food). His smile was just so contagious, and his laugh was pleasant to hear. He really made both me and my coworker want to be around him and dine in, which we did the last two nights we were there. Niko had to work on his birthday on April 27 too, so we felt bad he didn't get to be off... but that didn't change is wonderful attitude one bit! Great guy!

All in all, we both had a great stay because of these two. Now, if only the rest were as good as these two, it would have been a 5 star rating... these two gentleman made a difference!< /review>< pics>
